  `nextButtonText` varchar(30) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT 'Next',

  `dateModified` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,

  `triggerType` varchar(1) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,

--
-- Table structure for table `storage_patients`
--

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `storage_patients`;
/*!40101 SET @saved_cs_client     = @@character_set_client */;
/*!40101 SET character_set_client = utf8 */;
CREATE TABLE `storage_patients` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT 'primary key for patient, it will serve as our system''s patient Id',
  `programpatientId` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `sourcePatientId` varchar(45) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Id assigned to patient by source system - e.g Pat148R-2KD-BOS',
  `prefix` varchar(45) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'e.g. Mr, Dr., Ms, Sir, Princess, Knight, etc',
  `firstName` varchar(45) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'e.g. John',
  `middleName` varchar(45) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'e.g Joshua',
  `lastName` varchar(45) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'e.g. Doe',
  `suffix` varchar(45) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'e.g. Jr, III, IV etc.',
  `dob` datetime DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Patient''s date of birth 1-1-1912',
  `genderId` int(11) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Look up value from lu_Genders. Look up field is int and not free hand field because we should have some limits to some fields as what the user can type.  We will add it to our look up table if something creative comes up.  It is also a repetitive field, using int will take up less space and faster when it comes to indexing\nSample equivalent values are - male, female, unknown, transgender, etc.',
  `raceId` int(11) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Look up Id from lu_Races - equivalent values could be Asian, White, Black, etc.',
  `hispanicId` int(11) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'id from lu_Hispanics\nSample look up values are Yes, No, Not Reported',
  `primaryLanguageId` int(11) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Id from lu_Languages - Sample look up values - English, Spanish, Polish, Mandarin (Chinese), Cantonese (Chinese) etc.',
  `englishProficient` varchar(10) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'can be Yes, No, Unknown...\nWe wi\nso changing it to varchar',
  `maritalStatusId` int(11) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'look up from lu_MartialStatuses - Sample look up values are - Single, Married, Divorced, Not Reported, etc.',
  `email` varchar(100) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'e.g. test@test.com',
  `additionalContactNumber` varchar(45) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `url` varchar(100) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'e.g. http://test.com',
  `occupation` varchar(45) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `guardianName` varchar(45) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'name of guardian - Jane Doe, John Smith',
  `emergencyContact` varchar(45) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Name of emergency contact - Jane Doe',
  `emergencyTel` varchar(45) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '123-456-7890',
  `patientStatusId` int(11) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'id from lu_PatientStatuses - Could be equivalent int value of active, pending, future, expired, etc.',
  `dateCreated` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP COMMENT 'This is the date that the record was added to UT',
  `race` varchar(45) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `lastContacted` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  `clientType` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `genderFK_idx` (`genderId`),
  KEY `raceFK_idx` (`raceId`),
  KEY `lauguageFK_idx` (`primaryLanguageId`),
  KEY `martialStatusFK_idx` (`maritalStatusId`),
  KEY `hispanicFK_idx` (`hispanicId`),
  KEY `patientFK_idx` (`programpatientId`),
  CONSTRAINT `genderFK` FOREIGN KEY (`genderId`) REFERENCES `lu_genders` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `hispanicFK` FOREIGN KEY (`hispanicId`) REFERENCES `lu_hispanics` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `lauguageFK` FOREIGN KEY (`primaryLanguageId`) REFERENCES `lu_languages` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `martialStatusFK` FOREIGN KEY (`maritalStatusId`) REFERENCES `lu_maritalStatuses` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `patientFK` FOREIGN KEY (`programpatientId`) REFERENCES `programPatients` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `raceFK` FOREIGN KEY (`raceId`) REFERENCES `lu_races` (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=8 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 COLLATE=utf8_unicode_ci;
/*!40101 SET character_set_client = @saved_cs_client */;
